itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Introduction</h1><a id="user-content-introduction" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Introduction" href="#introduction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are the learning materials for the <strong>first practical video</strong> of the <strong>ThingsBoard CE course</strong>.
During this lesson, you will learn how to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Add your first <strong>asset</strong> with the corresponding <strong>attributes</strong>.</li>
<li>Create first <strong>dashboard</strong> with the <strong>custom Information card widget</strong>.</li>
<li>Personalize the <strong>dashboard</strong> and <strong>Card widget appearence</strong> with <strong>code</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding asset</h1><a id="user-content-adding-asset" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding asset" href="#adding-asset"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To add a new asset, go to the <strong>Entities</strong> section &gt; <strong>Assets</strong>, and then select the <strong><code>+</code></strong> icon &gt; <strong>Add new asset</strong>. Then enter the asset name and create the corresponding asset profile.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Name</th>
<th align="left">Asset profile</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left"><code>Office A</code></td>
<td align="left">office</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding attributes</h1><a id="user-content-adding-attributes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding attributes" href="#adding-attributes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To add a new attribute, select the office, go to the <strong>Attributes</strong> tab, and select the <strong><code>+</code></strong> icon. Enter the correspoding key, select the value type, and enter the value itself:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Key</th>
<th align="left">Value type</th>
<th align="left">Value</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left"><code>address</code></td>
<td align="left">String</td>
<td align="left">645 5th Ave, New York</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left"><code>floor</code></td>
<td align="left">Integer</td>
<td align="left">3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left"><code>email</code></td>
<td align="left">String</td>
<td align="left"><a href="mailto:office.a@mail.test">office.a@mail.test</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left"><code>phone</code></td>
<td align="left">String</td>
<td align="left">+1 121 333 4455</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left"><code>officeManager</code></td>
<td align="left">String</td>
<td align="left">Emma Johnson</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuring Information card widget</h1><a id="user-content-configuring-information-card-widget" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuring Information card widget" href="#configuring-information-card-widget"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To customize the Information card widget with code:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Navigate to the <strong>Appearance</strong> tab and paste the code in the corresponding <strong>Markdown/HTML pattern</strong> window:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Information on office
 - **Address**: ${address}
 - **Floor**: ${floor:0}
 - **Office manager**: ${officeManager}
 - **Phone**: ${phone}
 - **Email**: ${email}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code># Information on office
 - **Address**: ${address}
 - **Floor**: ${floor:0}
 - **Office manager**: ${officeManager}
 - **Phone**: ${phone}
 - **Email**: ${email}

</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">To further beautify the widget, turn on the <strong>Use markdown/HTML value function</strong> option. In the corresponding window, add the value function:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="if (data.length) {

                                '&lt;span class="attribute_label"&gt;Floor&lt;/span&gt;' +
                            '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="attribute_container"&gt;' +
                            '&lt;div class="icon_wrapper"&gt;' +
                                '&lt;tb-icon class="icon" color="primary" matButtonIcon&gt;person&lt;/tb-icon&gt;' +
                            '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                            '&lt;div class="attribute_content"&gt;' +
                                `&lt;p class="attribute"&gt;${information.officeAttributesField.officeManager}&lt;/p&gt;` +
                                '&lt;span class="attribute_label"&gt;Office manager&lt;/span&gt;' +
                            '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;/div&gt;' +
                        '&lt;div class="attribute_container"&gt;' +
                            '&lt;div class="icon_wrapper"&gt;' +
                                '&lt;tb-icon class="icon" color="primary" matButtonIcon&gt;call&lt;/tb-icon&gt;' +

                            '&lt;div class="attribute_content"&gt;' +
                                `&lt;p class="attribute"&gt;${information.officeAttributesField.phone}&lt;/p&gt;` +

</code></pre></div>

<li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Setting dashboard background image</h1><a id="user-content-setting-dashboard-background-image" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Setting dashboard background image" href="#setting-dashboard-background-image"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To add a new background image:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Select the <strong>Layouts</strong> &gt; <strong>Gear</strong> icon.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">In the <strong>Background image</strong> section, select <strong>Browse from gallery</strong> &gt; <strong>Upload image</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Drag &amp; drop the image or upload it from your computer.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The <a href="/thingsboard/learning-materials/blob/main/resources/office-room.jpg">image</a> we use in this tutorial.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Save the changes.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Customizing dashboard appearence</h1><a id="user-content-customizing-dashboard-appearence" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Customizing dashboard appearence" href="#customizing-dashboard-appearence"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To customize the dashboard appearence:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Select the <strong>Settings</strong> icon and go to the <strong>Advanced settings</strong> section.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">In the <strong>Dashboard CSS</strong> section, paste the following code:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=".tb-widget-container &gt; .tb-widget {
    border-radius: 8px;
    box-shadow: 0px 4px 10px rgba(23, 33, 90, 0.5);
}"><pre class="notranslate"><code>.tb-widget-container &gt; .tb-widget {
    border-radius: 8px;
    box-shadow: 0px 4px 10px rgba(23, 33, 90, 0.5);
}
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Save the changes.</p>
</li>
</ul>

      .user-mention[href$="/naidamariia"]:before,
      .user-mention[href$="/naidamariia"]:after {
        content: '';
        display: inline-block;
        width: 2px;
      }
    </style>


    </div>
